SAC TYPIC/AMBUD/Operational

AMTRIGON-8 (201-283995), AMBUD Case #97

ACTAN REQUIRED. ANCIENCES

Reference:

UFGW-7040, 29 April 1968

AMTRIGON-8 was a member of the VILLARO crew.

During

May 1962 he clandestinely and without authorization boarded an

infiltration craft moments before its departure on an

operational mission.

absence was not discovered until the

team had infiltrated and moved into its first position.

on 8 or 9 June 1962 the Intiltration team, including

AMTRIGON-8,

became engaged in a firefight with a militia

or perhaps captured.

However, no further word has been heard

from ANTRIGON-8 and he is presumed to be dead.

Taking into consideration that the disposition of this

could have an affect on the morale of the other crew

members and their attitude toward worthi,

it was decided to

advise the widow of AMTRIGON:8 that he died a hero's death--

while fighting for the liberation of his country and to continue

monthly payments to the widow and children for an indefinite

Inclusion of Subject's name

on AMBUD Hero & Martyr

was deemed to be the most suitable and expeditlous manner

in which to handle such payments.

4.

The response to paragraph 2 of reference will be

the subject of a separate dispatch.

Distribution:

AMTIKI-I has contacted the bank regarding the Social

Security numbers requested and has been advised that, although

the bank is not obligated to insist upon Social Security or other

identifying numbers for these accounts, it does feel that AlrIKI-1

may ultimately be subjected to an inquiry

the Internal Revenue

Their reasoning is based primarily upon the fact that

the accounts,

while trust accounts for our

purposes, are not true

trust accounts in that no trust agreements

are of record at the

(Trust agreements could

of course, since the

individuals were not and are not avallable to sign.)

In order to protect ANTIKI-1 from any possible IRS

investigation and, rather than pursue the matter further with the

bank, for which we have.

these accounts be closed out over a two or three month period and

re-established at Headquarters through the appropriate DTEARN

channels.

If the accounts remain here, it will be necessary to

new signature cards for each account removing Humphrey O.

TIMANUS as a signatory and adding a JMCOBRA asset as an "inside"

trustee for control purposes, or to remove ANTIKI-1 entirely and

establish the JNCOBRA asset

as the sole trustee.

3. Please advise.

Lears Bi Hellaris

TRANSLATION

Havana, 17 August 1967

COCONUT GROVE. BANK

MIANI, FLORIDA

Sir:

Attention: Mr. Administrator

I am writing to you to ask you to do me the favor of informing

Nr. John Poulbath

that I urgently need him to contact me because

I want him to send the passages to me to go (to the U.S.) via Spain.

The reason I have taken the llberty of writing is that in

Novumber of last year, I wrote to Mr.

Paulbath at PO Box 127, Tamiam

Station in that city and after almost six months the letter was

returned to me with the notation that the address was not registered.

Since

that timo a triend of mine who lives in Los Angeles has veen

trying to locate him and to date hos had no success.

Mr: Paulboth sent me a notice informing that the monthly stipend

due me (os a

death of my husband)

per dotal policy 1023,.

was being deposited in

that bank, enclosed is that notice.

last news. I lad from Mr. Paulbath was in February 1966 when he inforned

me that on that date the account showed a balance of US $12, 518.21.

I appcal to your kindness for help, since I have been trying

for more than

six

years since my husband died R.I.P. to leave (Cuba).

I adanos almost had all my papers in order to leave when the American

Erbassy was closed that was two months after my husband had departed

(Cuba),

later

that same year came the Bay of Pigs Invasion

and my husband was killed.

On 1 June my daughter was,

had the visa cond not eve bocatso i had not denn ante to set

total prits

a passport for my daughter since to obtain it they demanded my husband's

death certificate and his death was not recorded in any court, I went

to all the places it could have been recorded.

Then I began to visit

lawyers and government offices to find out how I could obtain a passport

for my daughter.

After much fighting,

it was delivered to me at the

end of November

of last year.

I immediately wrote to Sir. Paulbath

to ask

that he send me the money for passages right away and that was

the letter that was returned to me.

Since letters from there to here take so long,

I request that.

you

tell Mr. Paulbath to send me the money for passages

for, those,

indicatod below:

Concepcion PASTRANA Cernuda

Serafin CERNUDA Garcia

(US $154.00)

(US $308.00)

Graciela CERWUDA Fernandez

Maria CERNUDA Fernandez

(US $308.00)

and also tell him that the money for all should be sent to the

following address:

Colina #33, Jesus del Monte, Habana, Cuba.

TRANSLATION

Chicago, May 8, 1967

Dear Mr. -

In your letter of 1 Nay 1967 you asked me for my

marriage.

certificato and my son's birth certificate, I do not have them

because my home was immediately intervened by the so-called

Comandante Felix Torres who burned my family passport and wouldn't

even let me get my son's clothing. My cousin (?), Porilrio's

brother Rodolfo RAMIREZ same clandestinely went to the coasts of

Cuba to get me. I am sending you photostatic copios of our .

parolee cards. I belleve they will suffico but at tho samo time

I will write to Porfirio's mother who is still in Cuba since

she has not becn given permission to cave and come to this country

and I will ask her to get copies of the marriage certificato.

I will send them to you as soon as I receive them.

Thanks again,

/s/ Clara DELGADO

## Page 281

CUBAN DEMOCRATIC REVCLUTIONARY FRONT

FINANCE DEPARTMENT

RESUME OF THE INCOME AND EXPENSES OPERATIONS

"PAULA AND SOSA"

October 1 to 31, 1960

In the financial statements and annex the analysis and sub-analysis of

each one of the income and liabilities during the month of October are

shown.

Receipts, Invoices, deposit

slips and other papers are kept in our files.

As shown on Annex "I-D", a Revolving Fund has been created for the M1l1-

tary Section, amounting to the sume of $10, 000.00, divided into two parts

of $5,000.00

each, the amount of $3,387.81, was reinbursed to this Revoly

1ng Fund, as per Annex "I-D".

The amount of $50,000.00 which appears as "Transferenceg" in Annex I-M

corresponds to the transfered amount from the account of "Paula and Sosal

to "Rasco and Paula" account.

From this amount, we have paid in advance the November payment of the

military dependants.

In relation to "Checks to Justify", amounting to $69, 288.52, as per -

Annex "I-P", these could be classified in two groups; one formed by -

those corresponding to amounts advanced accoiding to budget to the

different Committees and Delegations and the other, formed by certain

expenses to be made, but specifically determined, with receipts dully

signed. The later could have been distributed to those accounts with

In the cassification, thus eliminating them from the title "to justify",

but have been kept as so, to be sure of the making of this expense for

the purpose to which the checks were drown for, or its actual classific-

ation, if these expense were made for other purposes than those original-

ly aimed to. This is due to the fact that some checks were drawn for a

specific purpose; they could also have been applied to acquire some

other asset, thus appearing at the end of the month a aise balance, since

It would appear as an expense, what it actually is an asset.

Section designated as "Transferences" $50, 000.00 1s compensule with an

Income for the same alount, when making a transference of funds to the

"Pasco and Paula" account to pay through it the payroll of the Military

Dependants, but through a mistake it was deposited again In the same

account.
